Miyazaki City, Miyazaki Prefecture
The rain clouds seem to have drifted into Miyazaki and it is raining at a blustery level.
It looks like the rain in Kyushu will continue for a little while longer.
We have received comments that the rain clouds coming from the southwest have caused the rain to fall in torrents.
There are puddles of water on the roads, and the rainfall tends to accumulate around this time.
Some parts of Kyushu are experiencing record rainfall. There is a possibility of more heavy rainfall tomorrow, so please remain vigilant.
We have read the reports we have received.
We need to be aware of flooding in many areas tomorrow as well.
Let‚Äôs take a look at this here.
This is about evacuation from flooded areas.
We are now in the night time, so if you are going to evacuate, you need to pay attention to these points.
Please wear comfortable clothes for evacuation. Put your belongings in a backpack so that you can use both hands freely. Make sure to wear athletic shoes because boots are difficult to walk in when water enters. If you evacuate tomorrow, please wear comfortable clothes.
Next, I would like to remind you that the force of the water is much greater than you think, and it is very dangerous.
The overflowing water is much stronger than you think, and it is difficult to walk when the water is knee-deep.
As an emergency evacuation, staying in a tall, sturdy building is one of the options.
We have also sent you a ‚ÄúFlooding Risk Estimate‚Äù so that you can check how high and deep the flooding will be in your area.
The third point is the following.
When flooded, you cannot see the road and it is very dangerous.
Flooded water is brownish and muddy, and you may not be able to see the borders of roads or manholes. If you have no choice but to move along flooded roads, please use a stick (umbrella, branch, walking stick, etc.) to check your footing as you go.
Also, please refrain from acting alone, and evacuate together with your neighbors or family members. It is also dangerous to drive a car, so please refrain from doing so.
The following are some tips on how to evacuate.
You can also check the latest information from the app.
Let‚Äôs take a look at the useful contents on the Rain News page. ‚ÄúLet‚Äôs take a look at some of the useful contents on the Rain News page:‚ÄùFlooding Risk Prediction.
The AI predicts flood damage based on the amount of precipitation expected for the next four days. You can use this page to see the current situation in your area.
This page is equipped with a GPS function, so you can view it here.
Now, let‚Äôs take a look at the areas in western Japan that are still at risk.
The area in red is the risk of flooding, and the height of the shin. The area where the water level may rise to this level is shown in red.
There is a possibility that this will happen tomorrow in Kumamoto City, Kumamoto Prefecture, so I would like to ask you to continue to be careful.
I would like you to proceed with evacuation based on the risk prediction.
Thank you for visiting the ‚ÄúWeather News‚Äù application.
Now, I would like to ask Mr.¬†Yamaguchi of the Forecast Center for more detailed weather information. Thank you very much for your time. Yes, please.

Izakaya

Â±ÖÈÖíÂ±ã„ÅÆÁâπÂæ¥„ÅØ„ÄÅ„É°„Éã„É•„Éº„ÅÆÁ®ÆÈ°û„Åå„Å®„Å¶„ÇÇË±äÂØå„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ„Åä„Å´„Åé„Çä„ÄÅ„ÅäÂØøÂè∏„ÄÅÂà∫Ë∫´„ÄÅ„ÅÜ„Å©„Çì„ÄÅÁÑº„ÅçÈ≥•„Å™„Å©„ÄÅ‰ª£Ë°®ÁöÑ„Å™Êó•Êú¨È£ü„ÅåÊèÉ„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ„Åæ„Åü„ÄÅ„ÅäÈÖí„ÇÑ„Éá„Ç∂„Éº„Éà„ÅÆÁ®ÆÈ°û„ÇÇË±äÂØå„Å´ÊèÉ„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ„É°„Éã„É•„Éº„ÇÇÂÜôÁúü‰ªò„Åç„ÇÑ„Çø„Éñ„É¨„ÉÉ„Éà„ÅßÂìÅ„ÇíË¶ã„Å™„Åå„ÇâÈÅ∏„Å∂‰∫ã„Åå„Åß„Åç„ÄÅÂ§ñÂõΩ‰∫∫„ÇÇÊ≥®Êñá„Åó„ÇÑ„Åô„Åè„Å™„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

„Åæ„Åü„ÄÅÂ±ÖÈÖíÂ±ã„ÅØÊôÆÈÄö„ÅÆ„É¨„Çπ„Éà„É©„É≥„Çà„Çä„ÇÇÂÄ§ÊÆµ„ÅåÂÆâ„Åè„ÄÅÂÜÖË£Ö„ÇÇÂíåÈ¢®„Å™„ÅÆ„ÅßÊó•Êú¨„ÅÆÈõ∞Âõ≤Ê∞ó„ÇÇÊ•Ω„Åó„ÇÅ„ÄÅÊâãËªΩ„Å´„É™„Ç¢„É´„Å™Êó•Êú¨ÊñôÁêÜ„ÇíÊ•Ω„Åó„ÇÄ„Åì„Å®„ÅåÂá∫Êù•„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

If you ask foreigners visiting Japan ‚ÄúWhere is your favorite place in Japan?‚Äù, many of them will answer ‚Äòizakaya‚Äô. We Japanese also often visit izakaya. Izakaya offer all-you-can-drink plans and banquet plans, so they‚Äôare often used for dinner parties with many people.

Izakaya are characterized by a wide variety of menu items. Typical Japanese dishes such as onigiri (rice balls), sushi, sashimi, udon, and yakitori are available. There is also a wide variety of drinks and desserts on offer. You can choose from a menu with pictures or view the items on a tablet, making it easy for foreigners to order.

Izakaya are cheaper than restaurants, and the decor is Japanese, so you can enjoy a Japanese atmosphere and real Japanese food easily.

Starbucks
Êò®Âπ¥„ÅÆ6Êúà„Å´ÊâãË©±„ÅåÂÖ±ÈÄöË™û„Å®„Å™„ÇãÊó•Êú¨ÂõΩÂÜÖÂàù„ÅÆ„Äé„Çπ„Çø„Éº„Éê„ÉÉ„ÇØ„Çπ„ÄÄ„Çµ„Ç§„Éã„É≥„Ç∞„Çπ„Éà„Ç¢„ÅåÊù±‰∫¨„ÄÄÂõΩÁ´ãÂ∏Ç„Å´„Ç™„Éº„Éó„É≥„Åó„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Åì„ÅÆÂ∫óËàó„ÅØ„ÄÅËÅ¥ËÄÖÔºàËÅ¥Ë¶ö„Å´ÈöúÂÆ≥„Åå„Å™„ÅÑ‰∫∫Ôºâ„Å®ËÅ¥Ë¶ö„Å´ÈöúÂÆ≥„ÅÆ„ÅÇ„Çã‰∫∫„ÅÆÂæìÊ•≠Âì°„ÅåÂÖ±„Å´ÂÉç„Åç„ÄÅ‰∏ª„Å™„Ç≥„Éü„É•„Éã„Ç±„Éº„Ç∑„Éß„É≥ÊñπÊ≥ï„ÅØÊâãË©±„Çí‰ΩøÁî®„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

Â∫óËàó„ÅÆ„Ç≥„É≥„Çª„Éó„Éà„ÅØ‚ÄúInfinite Possibilities‚Äù(ÁÑ°Èôê„ÅÆÂèØËÉΩÊÄß)ËÅ¥Ë¶ö„Å´ÈöúÂÆ≥„ÅÆ„ÅÇ„Çã„Çπ„Çø„ÉÉ„Éï„ÇÑ„ÅäÂÆ¢Êßò„Å´„Å®„Å£„Å¶„ÄÅ„ÅÇ„Çä„ÅÆ„Åæ„Åæ„ÅÆËá™ÂàÜ„Åß„ÅÑ„Çâ„Çå„ÇãÂ†¥ÊâÄ„Åß„ÅÇ„Çä„ÄÅÈöúÂÆ≥„ÅÆ„ÅÇ„ÇãËã•ËÄÖ„Å´„Å®„Å£„Å¶Â§¢„ÇÑÊú™Êù•„ÇíÊèè„Åë„ÇãÂ†¥ÊâÄ„ÄÇ„Åù„Åó„Å¶„Åì„ÅÆÂ∫óËàó„ÇíË®™„Çå„ÅüË™∞„ÇÇ„ÅåÊñ∞„Åü„Å™Ê∞ó„Å•„Åç„ÇíÂæó„Çâ„Çå„ÇãÂ†¥ÊâÄ„Å´„Å™„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÇíÁõÆÊåá„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Çã„Åù„ÅÜ„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ

„Åì„ÅÆ„Çà„ÅÜ„Å´„ÄÅÂ§öÊßò„Å™‰∫∫„ÄÖ„ÅåËá™ÂàÜ„Çâ„Åó„ÅèÈÅé„Åî„Åó„ÄÅÊ¥ªË∫ç„Åß„Åç„ÇãÂ±ÖÂ†¥ÊâÄ„Åå„ÇÇ„Å£„Å®„Åü„Åè„Åï„ÇìÂ¢ó„Åà„Çã‰∏ñ„ÅÆ‰∏≠„Å´Â§â„Çè„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åè„Å®ËâØ„ÅÑ„Åß„Åô„Å≠„ÄÇ

In June of last year, the first Starbucks Signing store in Japan opened in Kokuritsu City, Tokyo Prefecture, where sign language is a common language. The store is staffed by both hearing and hearing-impaired employees, and uses sign language as the primary method of communication.

The concept of the store is ‚ÄúInfinite Possibilities,‚Äù a place where hearing-impaired staff and customers can be who they are, and where young people with disabilities can envision their dreams and futures, and a place where everyone who visits the store can gain new insights.

I hope that the world will change to become a place where more and more diverse people can live and work as themselves.

Nara-Deer
Êó•Êú¨„ÅÆË¶≥ÂÖâÂêçÊâÄ„ÅÆ‰∏Ä„Å§„Åß„ÅÇ„ÇãÂ•àËâØÂÖ¨Âúí„ÄÇÊØéÊó•„Åü„Åè„Åï„Çì„ÅÆË¶≥ÂÖâÂÆ¢„ÅåË®™„Çå„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÂ•àËâØÂÖ¨Âúí„Å´„ÅØÂÖ¨Âúí„Å´‰Ωè„Çì„Åß„ÅÑ„ÇãËá™ÁÑ∂„ÅÆÈπø„Åå„Åü„Åè„Åï„Çì„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇË¶≥ÂÖâÂÆ¢„ÅØÈπø„Åü„Å°„Å´ÈπøÁî®„ÅÆ„Åõ„Çì„Åπ„ÅÑ„Çí„ÅÇ„Åí„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÅåÂá∫Êù•„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÈπø„ÇÇË¶≥ÂÖâÂÆ¢„Åã„Çâ„Åõ„Çì„Åπ„ÅÑ„Çí„ÇÇ„Çâ„Åà„Çã‰∫ã„ÇíÁü•„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Çã„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅ„Åü„Åè„Åï„Çì„ÅÆÈπø„ÅåË¶≥ÂÖâÂÆ¢„Å´ÂØÑ„Å£„Å¶„Åç„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

„Åß„Åô„Åå„ÄÅ„Åì„ÅìÊï∞„É∂Êúà„ÅØ„Ç≥„É≠„Éä„Ç¶„Ç§„É´„Çπ„ÅÆÂΩ±Èüø„Åß„ÄÅË¶≥ÂÖâÂÆ¢„ÅåÊøÄÊ∏õ„Åó„Å¶„Åó„Åæ„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇÈπø„Åõ„Çì„Åπ„ÅÑ„ÇíÈ£ü„Åπ„Çã‰∫ã„ÅåÊ∏õ„Å£„ÅüÈπø„Åü„Å°„Åß„Åô„Åå„ÄÅ„Åì„Çå„ÅØÈπø„Å´„Å®„Å£„Å¶ËâØ„ÅÑ‰∫ã„Å†„Å£„Åü„Çà„ÅÜ„Åß„Åô„ÄÇÂÆü„ÅØÂ•àËâØÂÖ¨Âúí„ÅÆÈπø„Åü„Å°„ÅØÈπø„Åõ„Çì„Åπ„ÅÑ„ÅÆÈ£ü„ÅπÈÅé„Åé„Åß„ÅäËÖπ„ÇíÂ£ä„ÅóÊ∞óÂë≥„Å†„Å£„Åü„Çà„ÅÜ„Åß„Åó„Åü„ÄÇÂ∞ë„ÅóÊüî„Çâ„Åã„ÅÑ„Åµ„Çì„Çí„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åü„ÅÆ„Åß„Åô„ÄÇÈ£ü„ÅπÈÅé„Åé„Åå„Å™„Åè„Å™„Å£„ÅüÁèæÂú®„ÅØ„ÄÅÂÅ•Â∫∑ÁöÑ„Å™‰∏∏„Åè„Å¶Èªí„ÅÑ„Åµ„Çì„ÅåÂá∫„Çã„Çà„ÅÜ„Å´„Å™„Çä„ÄÅ„ÅäËÖπ„ÅÆË™øÂ≠ê„Åå„Çà„Åè„Å™„Å£„Åü„Çà„ÅÜ„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ

Nara Park is one of the most popular tourist attractions in Japan. It is visited by many tourists every day. In Nara Park, there are many natural deer that live in the park. Tourists can give crackers to the deer. The deer know that they can get crackers from tourists, so many of them come close to the tourists.

However, the number of tourists has decreased drastically in recent months due to the coronavirus. The deer have been eating fewer rice crackers, but this seems to have been a good thing for them. In fact, the deer in Nara Park seemed to have an upset stomach due to eating too many rice crackers. They were a little soft and lumpy. Now that they have stopped overeating, they produce healthy round and black feces, and their stomachs seem to have improved.

Monkeys-Spring

ÁèæÂú®„ÇÇ„Éã„Éõ„É≥„Ç∂„É´„Åü„Å°„Åå‰Ωì„ÇíÊ∏©„ÇÅ„Çã„Åü„ÇÅ„Å´„ÄÅÊ∏©Ê≥â„Å´ÂÖ•„Çä„Å´„ÇÑ„Å£„Å¶„Åç„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ‰ªä„Åß„ÅØ‰∏ñÁïå‰∏≠„ÅÆ‰∫∫„ÄÖ„Å´ÊÑõ„Åï„Çå„ÄÅÂ§ö„Åè„ÅÆÁ†îÁ©∂ÂÆ∂„ÇÑÂÜôÁúüÂÆ∂„Å™„Å©„ÇÇÊ∏©Ê≥â„Å´ÂÖ•„ÇãÁåø„ÇíË¶≥ÂØü„Åó„Å´Âú∞ÁçÑË∞∑„ÇíË®™„Çå„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

In the northern part of Nagano Prefecture, there is Jigokudani in Joshinetsu Kogen National Park. It is located at an altitude of 850 meters on a plateau of snow and snow covered cliffs and valleys. This place is covered with snow for almost a third of the year. There are many natural hot springs there.

Humans are not the only ones who have discovered these natural hot springs. In the early 1960s, Japanese monkeys came down from the high forests above the canyon and started using the hot springs to warm themselves.

Even today, Japanese monkeys still come to take a bath in the hot spring to warm up their bodies. Many researchers and photographers visit Jigokudani to observe the monkeys bathing in the hot springs.

„Äé„Å¶„Åî„Äè„ÅØ„ÅäÊâã‰ºù„ÅÑ„Å™„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅÈõáÁî®Èñ¢‰øÇ„ÅØ„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ„Å™„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅ‰ºöÁ§æÂì°„ÄÅ‰∏ªÂ©¶„ÄÅÂ≠ê„Å©„ÇÇ„Å™„Å©Ë™∞„Åß„ÇÇÂá∫Êù•„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ‰ºöÁ§æÂì°„ÅÆÁî∑ÊÄß„Åå‰ªï‰∫ã„ÅÆÂêàÈñì„Å´ÈñãÂ∫óÊ∫ñÂÇô„ÇíÊâã‰ºù„Å£„Åü„Çä„ÄÅÂ∞èÂ≠¶Áîü„ÅÆÂ•≥„ÅÆÂ≠ê„Åå„Ç§„Çπ„ÇÑ„ÉÜ„Éº„Éñ„É´„ÅÆÊéÉÈô§„ÇíÊâã‰ºù„ÅÜ„Åì„Å®„Åå„Åß„Åç„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

È£üÂ†Ç„ÅÆÂ∫ßÂ∏≠Êï∞„ÅØÔºëÔºëÂ∏≠„ÄÇ‰ªä„ÅØÔºë‰∫∫„Åß„ÅîÈ£Ø„ÇíÈ£ü„Åπ„Çã‰∫∫„ÅåÂ§ö„ÅÑ„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅÁü•„Çâ„Å™„ÅÑÂÆ¢ÂêåÂ£´„Åß„ÇÇË©±„ÅåÂá∫Êù•„Å¶„ÄÅÊ•Ω„Åó„ÅèÈ£ü„Åπ„Çå„ÇãÈ£üÂ†Ç„Å´„Å™„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

Ponta," a diner with an unusual system, has opened in Okayama City, where people can get 800 yen worth of meal coupons if they help out at the restaurant for one hour. In the Okayama dialect, helping is called ‚ÄúTego,‚Äù and this diner calls it the "Tego System.

Since ‚ÄúTego‚Äù is a helping hand, there is no employment relationship. Therefore, anyone can do it, including office workers, housewives, and children. A company employee can help with the opening preparations in between work, or an elementary school girl can help clean the chairs and tables.

The cafeteria has 11 seats. Nowadays, many people eat dinner alone, so the cafeteria is a place where customers who don‚Äôt know each other can talk and enjoy eating together.

Chanko-Hot-Pot
ÂÜ¨„ÅÆÂØí„ÅÑÊó•„ÅØ„ÄÅÈçãÊñôÁêÜ„ÇíÈ£ü„Åπ„Å¶‰Ωì„ÇíÊ∏©„ÇÅ„Åü„Åè„Å™„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÈçãÊñôÁêÜ„ÅÆ‰∏Ä„Å§„Åß„ÅÇ„Çã„Å°„ÇÉ„Çì„ÅìÈçã„ÅØ„ÄÅ„ÅäÁõ∏Êí≤„Åï„Çì„ÅåÊØéÊó•È£ü„Åπ„ÇãÊñôÁêÜ„Å®„Åó„Å¶Áü•„Çâ„Çå„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

„ÅäÁõ∏Êí≤„Åï„Çì„ÅØ„Åì„ÅÆ„Å°„ÇÉ„Çì„ÅìÈçã„ÇíÈ£ü„Åπ„Å¶„ÄÅÂ§ß„Åç„Å™‰Ωì„Çí‰Ωú„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ„ÅäÁõ∏Êí≤„Åï„Çì„ÅØ„ÅÑ„Å£„Å±„ÅÑÈ£ü„Åπ„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÇÇ‰øÆË°å„ÅÆ‰∏Ä„Å§„Åß„Åô„ÄÇÂ§ß„Åç„Å™‰Ωì„Çí‰Ωú„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÅØ„ÅäÁõ∏Êí≤„Åï„Çì„Å´„Å®„Å£„Å¶„Å®„Å¶„ÇÇÂ§ßÂàá„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ„ÅäÁõ∏Êí≤„Åï„Çì„ÅØ„Å°„ÇÉ„Çì„ÅìÈçã„Çí‰∏º„ÅßÔºëÔºêÊùØ„Åè„Çâ„ÅÑÈ£ü„Åπ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

„Äå„Å°„ÇÉ„Çì„Äç„Å®Ë®Ä„ÅÜ„ÅÆ„ÅØ„Äå„ÅäÁà∂„Åï„Çì„Äç„Å®Ë®Ä„ÅÜÊÑèÂë≥„Åß„ÄÅ„Äå„Åì„Äç„ÅØÂ≠ê‰æõ„ÅÆÊÑèÂë≥„Åß„Åô„ÄÇÂ≠ê‰æõ„Å®‰∏ÄÁ∑í„Å´È£ü„Åπ„ÇãÈçã„Åß„ÄÅÈçã„ÅÆ‰∏≠„Å´„ÅØ„ÅÑ„Çç„Çì„Å™ÈáéËèú„ÇÑÈ≠ö„ÄÅËÇâ„Å™„Å©„ÅåÂÖ•„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÂë≥„ÅÆÁ®ÆÈ°û„ÇÇ„Åü„Åè„Åï„Çì„ÅÇ„Çä„ÄÅÈ£Ω„Åç„Çã‰∫ã„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ

On cold winter days, we like to eat hot pot dishes to warm ourselves up. Chanko-nabe, one of the hot pot dishes, is known as a dish that sumo wrestlers eat every day.

Sumo wrestlers build their big bodies by eating chanko-nabe. Eating a lot of food is part of the training for sumo wrestlers. Building a big body is very important for sumo wrestlers. Sumo wrestlers eat about 10 bowls of chanko-nabe.

The word ‚Äúchan‚Äù means ‚Äúfather‚Äù and ‚Äúko‚Äù means "child. It is a nabe that is eaten with children, and the nabe is filled with various vegetables, fish, and meat. There are many different flavors to choose from, so you will never get bored.

Bald Eagle, Grand Teton National Park, Wyoming, USA Widely distributed across the North American continent, the bald eagle is the national bird of the United States. It is featured on the U.S. national emblem and on the insignia of various organizations, and was the mascot of the Los Angeles Olympics as Eagle Sam‚Ä¶.

The bald eagle is a large bird with a wingspan of over two meters. It usually lives near water and uses its talons to catch fish. It was classified as endangered in 1967 due to deforestation and overfishing, but it has since recovered and is now off the endangered list.

Â∞æ„Å≥„Çå„ÇíÊµ∑Èù¢„Åã„ÇâÁ™Å„ÅçÂá∫„Åô„ÄÅÔΩ¢„Çª„Ç§„É™„É≥„Ç∞ÔΩ£„Å®Âëº„Å∞„Çå„ÇãË°åÂãï„ÅØ„ÄÅ„ÉüÔæÖ„Éü„Çª„Éü„ÇØ„Ç∏„É©ÁâπÊúâ„ÅÆ„ÇÇ„ÅÆ„ÄÇ‰ªñ„ÅÆ„ÇØ„Ç∏„É©„ÅÆ„Çà„ÅÜ„Å´„ÄÅÂ∞æ„Å≥„Çå„ÅßÊ∞¥Èù¢„ÇíÂè©„Åè„ÅÆ„Åß„ÅØ„Å™„Åè„ÄÅÊµ∑Èù¢„Å´ÈÄÜÁ´ã„Å°„Å´„Å™„Å£„ÅüÂΩ¢„ÅßÂ∞æ„Å≥„Çå„ÇíÂ∏Ü„ÅÆ„Çà„ÅÜ„Å´È´ò„ÅèÊé≤„Åí„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÊ∞óÂåñÁÜ±„Åß‰Ωì„ÇíÂÜ∑„ÇÑ„Åô„Åü„ÇÅ„ÄÅ„Å®„ÇÇË®Ä„Çè„Çå„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„Åå„ÄÅ„Åù„ÅÆÁêÜÁî±„ÅØ„ÅØ„Å£„Åç„Çä„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ

Southern Right Whale (Eubalaena japonica) tail fin off Hermanus, South Africa This is off the coast of Hermanus, South Africa. These waters are known as one of the best whale watching areas in the world. This tail fin belongs to the southern right whale. It is said that there are about 10,000 of them living throughout the southern hemisphere‚Ä¶

The behavior called ‚Äúsailing,‚Äù in which the tail fin sticks out of the water, is unique to southern right whales. Instead of striking the surface of the water with its tail fin as other whales do, it stands upright on the surface of the sea and holds its tail fin high like a sail. It is said that they do this to cool their bodies with the heat of vaporization, but the reason for this is not clear.

A lily-of-the-valley perching on a sunflower. This photo shows a lily-of-the-valley in the Americas. They migrate north in April and May, and south in September and October. Migration takes place mainly at night, and some studies suggest that they rely on the stars to determine their direction‚Ä¶

During the migration season, their small bodies make the long journey across the Gulf of Mexico, a distance of more than 1,000 kilometers. The lorikeet makes a short "Tsk! in short. Their main source of food is insects during the summer and plant seeds during the winter. Its population is increasing due to deforestation and agricultural land use, and stray birds have been observed in Europe.

Harz Narrow Gauge Railway, Germany, Harz National Park Today is the ‚ÄúBig Cold‚Äù. It is the coldest day of the year on the calendar. It is also the day when the cold training sessions are held and the sake is brewed‚Ä¶

The Harz National Park is also covered with white snow, giving it a cold appearance, but it is one of the most popular tourist destinations in Germany. The steam locomotive of the Harz narrow-gauge railroad, as you can see, is also popular. It carries tourists on a route that goes north to south while enjoying the beautiful winter scenery.

Suspension Bridge on the Soƒça River, Triglav National Park, Slovenia Today is World Bicycle Day as designated by the United Nations. The photo shows cyclists crossing the suspension bridge over the Soƒça River in Triglav National Park, called the Isonzo River in Italian. The color of the water is described as ‚Äúemerald beauty‚Äù‚Ä¶

Triglav National Park is the only national park in Slovenia. It is named after Triglau, the highest peak in the Julian Alps. The Giulian Alps were named after Julius Caesar, who founded the city of Cividale del Friuli at its southern base. There used to be a glacier, but it has disappeared.

Polar Bear, Svalbard, Norway This photo shows a polar bear swimming in the cold. In Western countries, many people enjoy swimming in the cold during the winter, and some even hold cold swimming competitions as New Year‚Äôs charity events. You may think that polar bears don‚Äôt need to swim in the cold, but for polar bears, the icy winter is the best time to hunt‚Ä¶

Polar bears are very good swimmers, with their large paws equipped with paddles. They gently ambush seals in the water and kill their prey in an instant. Here in the Svalbard archipelago, it is often said that there are more bears than people, but polar bears are well protected and it is forbidden to look for them. We are very lucky to be able to see them.

ÊûúÁâ©„ÅÆÊó¨„Å®Áî£Âú∞„Å´„Çà„Å£„Å¶„ÄÅÊñ∞„É°„Éã„É•„Éº„ÅåÊ¨°„ÄÖ„Å®ÁôªÂ†¥„Åô„Çã„ÅÆ„ÇÇ„ÄÅ„Åì„ÅÆ„ÅäÂ∫ó„ÅÆÁâπÂæ¥„ÄÇ6ÊúàÊú´„Åã„Çâ„ÅØ„ÄÅÂÆÆÂè§Â≥∂„ÅÆËá™ÂÆ∂Ëæ≤Âúí„ÅßÊ†ΩÂüπ„Åó„Åü„Éû„É≥„Ç¥„Éº„ÅÆ„Åã„ÅçÊ∞∑„ÅåÁôªÂ†¥„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ„Åæ„Åü„ÄÅ„Éü„É´„ÇØ„ÇÑ„É®„Éº„Ç∞„É´„Éà„ÇíËøΩÂä†„Åó„Å¶„ÅäÂ•Ω„Åø„Åß„Ç´„Çπ„Çø„Éû„Ç§„Ç∫„Åß„Åç„ÇãÊ•Ω„Åó„Åï„ÇÇ„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

Â§ïÊñπ5ÊôÇ‰ª•Èôç„ÅØÊØîËºÉÁöÑÊ∑∑Èõë„ÅåÂ∞ë„Å™„Åè„ÄÅ‰∏¶„Å∞„Åö„Å´ÂÖ•„Çå„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÇÇ„ÄÇË°åÂàó„ÅåÈï∑„Åè„Å™„Å£„ÅüÂ†¥Âêà„ÄÅÊï¥ÁêÜÂà∏„ÅåÈÖç„Çâ„Çå„Çã„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅÂæÖ„Å°ÊôÇÈñì„ÇíÂà©Áî®„Åó„Å¶Ë®™„Çå„Åü„ÅÑÂë®Ëæ∫„ÅÆË∞∑Ê†πÂçÉ„Çπ„Éù„ÉÉ„Éà„Çí‰∫ãÂâç„Å´„ÉÅ„Çß„ÉÉ„ÇØ„Åó„Å¶„Åä„Åè„Å®„ÅÑ„ÅÑ„Åß„Åô„Çà„ÄÇ

Soft and fluffy shaved ice made with natural ice and overflowing with homemade honey at the popular ‚ÄúHimitsu-do‚Äù store in Yanaka

As we wait for the rainy season to end, the season for shaved ice has finally arrived!„ÄÄHimitsu-do, located in Yanaka, a downtown area of Tokyo, is a very popular shaved ice store where people line up to get their shaved ice, which is made from natural ice shaved by hand and drizzled with homemade honey. To date, more than 130 types of shaved ice have been added to the menu, and the number continues to grow. Here are some of the shaved ice dishes you should try this summer.

A five-minute walk from JR Nippori Station. A five-minute walk from JR Nippori Station, down the famous ‚ÄúYuyake Dan Dan‚Äù street, and into a small alley, you will see a building with a red door that is Himitsu-do. Regardless of the season, the line that forms before the store opens is one of Yanaka‚Äôs specialties. During the summer vacations, it is common to wait for an hour or two.

The secret of its deliciousness is that the ice and honey are handmade. The natural ice, which grows slowly in the natural cold, comes from the ‚ÄúMitsuhoshi Himuro‚Äù in Nikko. The ice is shaved manually in the traditional way to create a texture that melts on the tongue. The syrup made from seasonal fruits is called ‚Äúnectar‚Äù here, and it is all homemade without additives. The combination of natural ice, hand shaved ice, and homemade honey is what creates the perfect shaved ice that you will want to eat all year round.

When it comes to shaved ice, strawberries are always the best! When it comes to shaved ice, strawberries are the most popular. The strawberry menu item that is popular here regardless of the season is called ‚ÄúSecret Strawberry Miruku‚Äù (1,300 yen). The strawberry milkshake is made from only seasonal ripe strawberries grown by partner farmers in Shizuoka and Akita prefectures, and is so thick that it spills out of the glass. The strawberry honey is so thick that it spills out of the glass.

When you take a bite, after the slightly thick texture, the sweet and sour taste of the strawberries and the coolness of the ice come together to fill your mouth. It is also important to note that only one side of the ice is covered with honey. Even if you only eat the ice, you can still taste the rich flavor of the shaved ice at Himitsu-do. Please try the natural ice itself, which is crisp and cold but has a gentle flavor.

A seasonal menu item available until August is the ‚ÄúMeron Zammai‚Äù (1,900 yen), made with melon honey directly from Ibaraki, Japan‚Äôs largest melon production area. The ripe melon fruit on top of the ice covered with so much honey gives the melon, also known as the ‚Äúking of fruits,‚Äù an appearance worthy of its name. The bottom of the ice is fluffy, so be careful not to drop the melon.

A slightly unique item on the menu is the ‚ÄúGolden Tomato‚Äù (1,300 yen). The sweetness of the tomatoes is so rich that it will change your image of tomatoes in salads, and it is a healthy dish that contains a lot of lycopene, which is said to be an excellent antioxidant. The dried tomato topping is from Italy. The topping is dried tomatoes from Italy, which have a gummy texture and a nice flavor.

Another feature of this restaurant is that new menu items are introduced one after another depending on the season and origin of the fruits, and since the end of June, shaved ice made from mangoes grown on their own farm in Miyakojima has been available. From the end of June, shaved ice made from mangoes grown in their own farm on Miyakojima Island is available, and you can customize it by adding milk or yogurt.

After 5:00 p.m., the place is relatively less crowded and you may be able to get in without waiting in line. If the line gets too long, numbered tickets will be handed out, so it‚Äôs a good idea to check out nearby Yanesen spots you want to visit beforehand to take advantage of the waiting time.

NASA-developed special shock-absorbing material disperses pressure; 3D zero gravity pillow ‚ÄúGUTNAP Zero Gravity Pillow Cool‚Äù.It‚Äôs a great pillow that absorbs shock. The pillow is made of a material that absorbs and disperses pressure without cracking even when an egg is pressed against it. If the pressure on the pillow is released, it will quickly recover. High restoring power! Makes it easy to turn over and supports a good night‚Äôs sleep. The overwhelming shock-absorbing power of the pillow becomes its restoring power, and the pillow quickly returns to its original shape when you turn over. If you turn over while the pillow is sinking, only your head remains still and your body twists, putting strain on your neck and shoulders. The Zero Gravity Pillow uses this restorative force to support smooth tossing and turning. Since each cube supports the head in three dimensions, the pillow changes its shape to match the movement of the head as it turns. The pillow fits your body perfectly and does not leave any gap between your neck and the pillow, supporting your sleeping comfort like a custom-made pillow. The Zero Gravity Pillow features a unique total of 24 air holes design in the center of the cube. In addition, the cube-cut structure inside the pillow provides unparalleled air permeability. The Gravity Pillow is designed with a total of 24 air holes in the center of the cube. We do not accept returns or refunds on products that are still under development.

The English Conversation Highway provides information on how to learn English and become a professional translator.

All articles are written by Akira, who has over 10 years of experience as a professional translator, in collaboration with native English speakers.

The purpose of English Conversation Highway is to

To provide information on how to solve problems related to learning English and how to improve your ability to communicate in English. To help people become financially and emotionally independent through the use of English, so that they can realize their dreams and create an ideal lifestyle that makes their family and others happy. These are my goals.

Our hope is that our readers will be able to acquire English without difficulty while working or doing housework, and that they will be able to achieve their ideal lifestyle.

In order to achieve this goal, we provide the following information so that 100% Japanese people born and raised in Japan can acquire English while living a social life in Japan.

Akira, the operator of this site, has experience in working holidays, studying abroad, job hunting in the US, and working for an IT company in the US.

Based on these experiences, we will also provide information for those who are interested in expanding overseas.

What kind of life do you want to lead when you become fluent in English?

I want to be able to travel overseas independently and enjoy travel freely.
I want to be an internationally active businessman.
I would like to work as an interpreter or translator in English.
I want to have a foreign lover.
I want to enjoy movies and books in English.
I want to move to a foreign country.
I want to be thought of as smart.
There are many things you can do.

I myself studied English because I wanted to work as a translator, and I was able to become an independent translator.

You too can make your dreams come true.

Translation (my main job) Akira Work Translation work is very popular as a job that can be done at home using a computer.

This is because you can adjust the amount of work and the hours you work, and if you polish your skills, you can earn a lot of money.

I myself have been making a living and supporting my family by working as a translator for more than ten years.

If you search the Internet, you will find many translation courses, which shows the popularity of translation.

However, despite its popularity, I bet very few people have ever met a professional translator who can make a living from translation work alone.

Â∞ÇÈñÄÁü•Ë≠ò„ÅåË∫´„Å´‰ªò„ÅÑ„Å¶„ÅÑ„Å™„ÅÑ„Åì„Å®„Å´„Å§„ÅÑ„Å¶„ÅØ„ÄÅ„Åü„Å®„Åà„Å∞ITÁøªË®≥Ë¨õÂ∫ß„Å™„Å©„Å®ÈäòÊâì„Å£„Å¶ÂÆ£‰ºù„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„ÇãË¨õÂ∫ß„Åß„ÇÇ„ÄÅIT„Å´„Å§„ÅÑ„Å¶Â≠¶„Åπ„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÅØÂü∫Á§é„ÅÆÂü∫Á§é„Åß„Åó„Åã„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ

„Åæ„Åü„ÄÅ3„ÅÆ‰ªï‰∫ã„ÇíÂßã„ÇÅ„ÇãÊñπÊ≥ï„Å´„Å§„ÅÑ„Å¶„ÅØ„ÄÅ„Åª„Å®„Çì„Å©„ÅÆË¨õÂ∫ß„ÅØ‰Ωï„ÇÇÊïô„Åà„Å¶„Åè„Çå„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ
‰∏≠„Å´„ÅØ„ÄÅË¨õÂ∫ß„ÅßÂÑ™ÁßÄ„Å™ÊàêÁ∏æ„ÇíÂèé„ÇÅ„Åü„ÇâÈÅãÂñ∂‰ºöÁ§æ„ÅÆ„Éà„É©„Ç§„Ç¢„É´„ÅåÂÖçÈô§„Åï„Çå„Çã„Å®„ÅÑ„ÅÜÁâπÂÖ∏„Åå‰ªò„ÅÑ„Å¶„ÅÑ„ÇãË¨õÂ∫ß„ÇÇ„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ
„Åó„Åã„Åó„ÄÅ‰ªï‰∫ã„ÅÆ‰æùÈ†º„Åå„ÅÇ„Çã‰øùË®º„ÅØ„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„Åó„ÄÅËá™ÂàÜ„Åß‰ªï‰∫ã„Çí„Å®„Çã„Çπ„Ç≠„É´„ÇíË∫´„Å´‰ªò„Åë„Å™„Åë„Çå„Å∞„ÄÅÁøªË®≥ËÄÖ„Å®„Åó„Å¶Ëá™Á´ã„Åô„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÅØ‰∏çÂèØËÉΩ„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ

Why there are so few translators

These translation courses should be designed so that when people who meet the requirements take the course, they should have the skills necessary to work and be able to start working when they finish the curriculum.

However, as a practical matter, very few people are able to start working when they complete the course.

There are multiple reasons for this, but the main reasons are

Not enough language skills have been acquired
Lack of specialized knowledge
They don‚Äôt know how to get a job.
The main reasons are

Lack of sufficient linguistic skills is due to lack of adequate guidance.
In order to acquire translation skills that can be used on the job, you need to receive thorough correction and guidance from someone with the skills of a professional translator.
However, since hiring professional translators is expensive in terms of labor costs, most courses only provide corrections according to the correction manual or only a few times.

As for the lack of specialized knowledge, for example, even if a course is advertised as an IT translation course, what you can learn about IT is only the basics.
Studying IT in a translation course is not enough to acquire enough expertise to work in that field.

Also, most courses don‚Äôt teach you anything about how to start a career in 3.
Some of the courses have a special offer that if you do well in the course, you will be exempted from the management company‚Äôs trial.
However, there is no guarantee that you will be offered a job, and unless you have the skills to get work on your own, it is impossible to be independent as a translator.

„Åü„Å®„Åà„Å∞„ÄÅ„Éó„É≠ÁøªË®≥ËÄÖ„Å´Ê∑ªÂâäÊåáÂ∞é„ÇÑË≥™Âïè„Å∏„ÅÆÂØæÂøú„Çí„Åó„Å¶„ÇÇ„Çâ„Å£„Åü„Çâ„ÄÅÈ´ò„ÅÑ‰∫∫‰ª∂Ë≤ª„Åå„Åã„Åã„Çã„Åü„ÇÅËµ§Â≠ó„Å´„Å™„ÇãÂèØËÉΩÊÄß„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

„Åæ„Åü„ÄÅÂ∞ÇÈñÄÁü•Ë≠ò„ÇíË∫´„Å´‰ªò„Åë„Å¶„ÇÇ„Çâ„ÅÜÂøÖË¶Å„Åå„ÅÇ„Çã‰∏ä„Å´„ÄÅÁøªË®≥„Åù„ÅÆ„ÇÇ„ÅÆ„Å®„ÅØÈñ¢‰øÇ„Å™„ÅÑÂñ∂Ê•≠„ÅÆÊñπÊ≥ï„Åæ„ÅßÊåáÂ∞é„Åô„ÇãÂøÖË¶Å„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

„Åï„Çâ„Å´Ë®Ä„Åà„Å∞„ÄÅÁøªË®≥ËÄÖ„Å®„Åó„Å¶ÂèéÂÖ•„ÇíÁ∂≠ÊåÅ„Åô„Çã„Åü„ÇÅ„Å´„ÄÅÂìÅË≥™„ÇíÁ∂≠ÊåÅ„Åô„Çã„Åü„ÇÅ„ÅÆ„Éé„Ç¶„Éè„Ç¶„ÇÑ„ÄÅÁîüÁî£ÊÄß„Çí‰∏ä„Åí„Çã„Åü„ÇÅ„ÅÆ„Éé„Ç¶„Éè„Ç¶„Åæ„ÅßÊïô„Åà„ÇãÂøÖË¶Å„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

Â∞ÇÈñÄÁöÑ„Å™Áü•Ë≠ò„Çí„Åü„Åè„Åï„ÇìÊåáÂ∞é„Åô„ÇãÂøÖË¶Å„Åå„ÅÇ„Çã„Åü„ÇÅ„ÄÅÁøªË®≥Ë¨õÂ∫ß„Åß„Åô„Åπ„Å¶Êïô„Åà„Çã„ÅÆ„Å´„ÅØÁÑ°ÁêÜ„Åå„ÅÇ„Çã„ÅÆ„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ

The original purpose of a translation course

The purpose of taking a course should not be ‚Äúto study translation‚Äù but "to be able to work in translation. And in order not to be swayed by the convenience of others, you need to be able to do everything by yourself, without depending on others or companies.

As I run a translation course, I believe that if I cannot lead you to that point, there is no point in having you take the course.

However, we understand that it is difficult to provide a course that can achieve this.

For example, if we had professional translators to correct and answer questions, we would have to pay high labor costs, which could result in a loss.

In addition, you need to provide them with specialized knowledge, and you also need to teach them sales methods that have nothing to do with translation itself.

In addition, we need to teach them how to maintain quality and increase productivity in order to maintain their income as translators.

It is impossible to teach everything in a translation course because it requires a lot of specialized knowledge.

„Åã„Å§„Å¶„ÅØÁßÅ„ÇÇ„ÄÅÁøªË®≥ËÄÖ„Å´„Å™„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÇíÂ§¢Ë¶ã„Å¶ÂãâÂº∑„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„ÅüÊôÇÊúü„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Åù„Çå„Å†„Åë„Å´„ÄÅ„Åù„ÅÜ„Åó„ÅüÁèæÂÆü„ÇíË¶ã„Çã„ÅÆ„ÅØÊÆãÂøµ„Åß‰ªïÊñπ„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ

„Åù„Åì„Åß„ÄÅ„Åì„ÅÆÁèæÂÆü„ÇíÂ§â„Åà„Çã„Åü„ÇÅ„Å´„ÄÅÁßÅ„ÅåË°åÂãï„Åô„Çã„Åì„Å®„Å´„Åó„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ

To avoid repeated setbacks

With over a decade of translation experience, I can teach you all this, but I was hesitant to put it into action.

I was hesitant to do so because the burden of support required for students to become independent was too great.

However, as it stands now, we are leaving people who have taken translation courses with great expectations and who really want to work as translators to repeatedly fall short of their goals.

There was a time when I, too, dreamed of becoming a translator and studied for a while. That‚Äôs why it‚Äôs a shame to see such a reality.

So, I decided to take action to change this reality.

From zero translation experience and no connections to becoming a professional translator

I myself went from having no translation experience, no connections, and no specialized knowledge to becoming an independent translator.

I can help others who are in the same situation as I was to become independent.

This is not possible with major courses because the cost is too high to make this happen. However, I can do everything myself, so I can do what I want without worrying about the cost.

Acquiring the skills to become an independent translator is not an easy task.

There will be times when you will feel frustrated.

However, if you share my views and are serious about wanting to work as a translator, I will do my best to support you.

To become an independent translator. Realize your ideal lifestyle.

‚ÄúTo be independent as a translator‚Äù and ‚ÄúTo realize your ideal lifestyle‚Äù are our goals.

From translator to "translator A translator, as I see it, is not someone who merely rephrases words, such as from English to Japanese or from Japanese to English.

A translator is not just a person who translates words from English to Japanese or Japanese to English, but a person who, through translation work, achieves an ideal lifestyle that allows him or her to be financially and emotionally independent, to realize his or her own dreams, and to make his or her family and others happy.

The job of translation has the potential to do just that, because it can be done without being restricted by anything, including time, place, age, or gender.

Therefore, I call people who agree with this idea ‚Äútayakusha,‚Äù meaning "people who make a leap in their lives through translation.

The Chinese character for ‚Äúleap‚Äù has the meaning of ‚Äúto leap high. The Chinese character for‚Äùleap" has the meaning of ‚Äúto leap high‚Äù or ‚Äúto move around vigorously,‚Äù and is used in words such as ‚Äúleap forward,‚Äù ‚Äúleap forward,‚Äù and "leap of courage.

My goal is to increase the number of translators who not only translate as a job, but also realize their ideal lifestyles with a view to the future.

I believe this is my mission as a translator.

Ëã±Ë™ûÂ≠¶Áøí„Å´„Åä„ÅÑ„Å¶„ÄÅ‰Ωï„Åã„ÅåÈñìÈÅï„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Çã„Åì„Å®„ÅØ„ÅÇ„Åç„Çâ„Åã„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ

How to Study English Women who study Most people who learn English face the problem of not being able to speak English no matter how much they study, or not being able to listen to native English speakers.

If you are reading this page, you have probably had the following experiences while studying English. I can‚Äôt improve my conversation even after studying with English conversation materials. I can‚Äôt speak English even though I‚Äôve memorized the grammar and vocabulary. Studying at an English conversation school does not improve my conversation. I can‚Äôt understand native English even though I listen to listening materials. Why do you have this experience?

The reason is not that you are not trying hard enough, that you are not talented in English, that you are not smart enough, or that you are too old too late.

It is due to the fact that wrong information about learning English is widely believed and you are studying based on wrong information.

For example, it is widely advertised that ‚Äúif you listen to English audio, you will naturally learn to speak English,‚Äù but have you ever actually seen even one such person?

Why is it that there are so many English conversation schools, including online English schools, but you don‚Äôt see many people who have learned to speak English?

It is obvious that there is something wrong in learning English.

What is the best way to learn English as an adult?

I often hear that when families go abroad, only the children become fluent in English, while the parents do not improve their English.

Children can absorb a foreign language relatively naturally because their brains are flexible, but it is impossible for them to acquire it naturally as adults.

Thus, it is said that the dividing line between being able to acquire a foreign language naturally is around the age of 12 to 13.

Therefore, adults who have passed this age need a study method for adults.

English Conversation (Speaking) Speaking Women The ‚ÄúSpeaking English‚Äù category focuses on phrases that are commonly used in everyday English conversation.

The phrases are all Eikaiwa Highway originals, written by native speakers.

We hope you will find these phrases useful and useful in your daily life.

Listening and Pronunciation Women in Listening The ‚ÄúListening and Pronunciation‚Äù category provides useful information for improving listening and pronunciation.

It‚Äôs full of useful content, including free listening sites and pronunciation exercises taught by professional interpreters.

Grammar Women Teaching English In the ‚ÄúGrammar‚Äù category, each article (or unit) is designed to be read in about 10 minutes, so that you can learn grammar from the basics.

Even those who failed at junior high school English find it easy to understand! It‚Äôs easy to understand!

English vocabulary Students learning words In the ‚ÄúEnglish Vocabulary‚Äù category, we explain some words that are difficult to use, explain how to remember them, and introduce some recommended vocabulary materials.

If you have trouble with words, please read on.

TOEIC Stairs In the ‚ÄúTOEIC‚Äù category, you can learn how to get a high score on TOEIC, the difference between successful and unsuccessful study methods, and recommended study materials.

If you are planning to take the TOEIC, please read on, as I, who scored 940 on TOEIC on my first attempt without studying for the exam, will tell you all about the ins and outs of TOEIC.

If you can‚Äôt find what you want to know, try searching in the search window.

„Åß„ÇÇ„ÄÅ‰Ωï„ÇíË©±„Åù„ÅÜ„Åã„Å™?  „Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØ‰∏ÄÁîüÊá∏ÂëΩËÄÉ„Åà„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ‰∏ÄÂàÜ„ÄÅ‰∏âÂàÜ„ÄÅ„Åù„Åó„Å¶ÂçÅÂàÜ„ÅåÁµå„Å°„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇÊ¨°„ÅÆÈßÖ„Åß„ÄÅ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØÈôç„Çä„Å™„Åë„Çå„Å∞„ÅÑ„Åë„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ„Å©„ÅÜ„Åó„Çà„ÅÜ?‰Ωï„ÇíË®Ä„Åä„ÅÜ?ÊôÇÈñì„Åå„Å™„ÅÑ„ÄÇÈõªËªä„ÅØÊ¨°„ÅÆÈßÖ„Å´Âà∞ÁùÄ„Åó„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ„Åù„ÅÆÂ•≥„ÅÆ‰∫∫„ÇÇÂêå„ÅòÈßÖ„ÅßÈôç„Çä„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØÊÄ•„ÅÑ„ÅßÈõªËªä„ÇíÈôç„Çä„Å¶„ÄÅÂ§ß„Åç„Å™Â£∞„Åß„Åù„ÅÆ‰∫∫„Å´Ë©±„Åó„Åã„Åë„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Äå„ÅÇ„ÅÆ„ÄÅ„Åì„Çì„Å´„Å°„ÅØ!„Äç„Åù„ÅÆ‰∫∫„ÅØËøî‰∫ã„Çí„Åó„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„Åß„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Åù„Åó„Å¶„ÄÅÊ≠©„ÅÑ„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åç„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ „Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØ„Åå„Å£„Åã„Çä„Åó„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Åù„Åó„Å¶„ÄÅ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØÊò†ÁîªÈ§®„Å´Ë°å„Åç„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅåÊò†ÁîªÈ§®„Å´ÁùÄ„ÅÑ„Åü„Å®„Åç„ÄÅ„Åù„ÅÆÂ•≥„ÅÆ‰∫∫„ÇÇÊò†ÁîªÈ§®„Å´„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØ„ÄÅ„Åù„ÅÆÂ•≥„ÅÆ‰∫∫„Å´„ÅÇ„ÅÑ„Åï„Å§„Çí„Åó„Çà„ÅÜ„Å®ÊÄù„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Åù„ÅÆ‰∫∫„ÅØ„ÄÅÂ≠óÂπï„ÅÆÊò†Áîª„ÇíË¶ã„Åü„ÅÑ„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅÊò†ÁîªÈ§®„ÅÆ„Çπ„Çø„ÉÉ„Éï„Å®Ë©±„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Åù„ÅÆ‰∫∫„ÅØ„ÄÅËÄ≥„Åå‰∏çËá™Áî±„Åß„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Å†„Åã„Çâ„ÄÅ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„Åå„ÅÇ„ÅÑ„Åï„Å§„Åó„Åü„Å®„Åç„ÄÅËÅû„Åì„Åà„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„Åß„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Åù„Åó„Å¶„ÄÅ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØ„Åù„ÅÆÂ•≥„ÅÆ‰∫∫„Å´ÊâãÁ¥ô„ÇíÊõ∏„Åç„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„Äå‰∏ÄÁ∑í„Å´Êò†Áîª„ÇíË¶ã„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„Åã?„Äç‰ªä„ÄÅ„Ç¢„É§„Ç≥„ÅØÊØéÊó•ÈõªËªä„Åß„Åù„ÅÆÂ•≥„ÅÆ‰∫∫„Å®„Éé„Éº„Éà„Å®„Éö„É≥„Çí‰Ωø„Å£„Å¶Êò†Áîª„ÅÆË©±„Çí„Åó„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

Ayako rides trains every day. When she goes to work, goes shopping, meets with friends, goes to an English-conversation lesson, or goes to the movies, she rides trains. When she goes to work on weekdays, Ayako always rides the same train every day with the same people. When she goes out on weekends, there are always different people on the train. Whenever Ayako rides a train, there is something she always wonders about. Where do these people come from and where do these people go? Today is June 15th and it is a Sunday morning. Summer is just around the corner. It is a nice day. Today, Ayako takes the train and goes to see a new movie. Ayako slowly looked around in the train. Because it is a Sunday morning, there are not many people riding it. In front of Ayako, there are a small boy and a young man sitting together. The boy is watching a video on a tablet. The young man is looking outside the window of the train. Are they a child and father? Or, are they a student and teacher? Next to Ayako, there is a woman sitting by herself. She is wearing a blue dress and sending a message to someone on her cellphone. Where is she going in a blue dress? Does she have a job interview? Or, is she going to her friend‚Äôs wedding? Ayako is looking around. There is someone that she has seen before. This woman is standing near a door and reading a book. When she goes to work, Ayako sees this woman every day. But she has never talked to her before. This woman is always reading a book. What do I do? Maybe I want to talk to her? But what should I talk about? Ayako is thinking about what to say very hard. One minute, three minutes, ten minutes have passed. She needs to get off at the next station. What do I do? What do I say? There is no time left. The train stops at the next station. And the woman also got off at the same station. Ayako got off the train hurriedly and got to talk to the woman in a loud voice. ‚ÄúUm, hello!‚Äù The woman did not answer to Ayako and just walked away. Ayako got disappointed. Ayako then went to the movie theater. When she arrived at the theater, that woman was also there. Ayako thought she was now going to say hi to her. The woman wanted to watch a subtitled movie so she was talking to a staff member of the theater. She was deaf. That‚Äôs why she could not hear it when Ayako said hi to her. Ayako then wrote a letter to the woman. ‚ÄúWould you like to watch a movie together?‚Äù Now Ayako and the woman talk about movies everyday on the train using a notebook and pen.

Mountaineer

ÁôªÂ±±ÂÆ∂„ÅØ„ÄÅÂ±±„Å´„ÅÇ„ÇãÂ∞èÂ±ã„ÅßÊöÆ„Çâ„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ‰∏Ä‰∫∫„ÅßÂÖÉÊ∞ó„Å´ÊöÆ„Çâ„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÊØéÊúù„ÄÅ‰∏âÊôÇÈñìÂ±±„ÇíÁôª„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ„Åù„Åó„Å¶„ÄÅÈáéËèú„ÇíËÇ≤„Å¶„Å¶„ÄÅÈ£ü„Åπ„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÁôªÂ±±ÂÆ∂„ÅØ„ÄÅÁóÖÈô¢„Å´Ë°å„Å£„Åü„Åì„Å®„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ„Å®„Å¶„ÇÇÂÖÉÊ∞ó„Å™„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅÁóÖÊ∞ó„Å´„Å™„Å£„Åü„Åì„Å®„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ‰ªäÊó•„ÇÇÊòº„Å´„Ç≠„Éé„Ç≥„Çí„Å®„Çä„Å´Ë°å„Åç„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÁôªÂ±±ÂÆ∂„ÅØ„ÄÅ„Ç≠„Éé„Ç≥„Å´„Å§„ÅÑ„Å¶„Çà„ÅèÁü•„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÈ£ü„Åπ„Çâ„Çå„Çã„Ç≠„Éé„Ç≥„Å®È£ü„Åπ„Çâ„Çå„Å™„ÅÑ„Ç≠„Éé„Ç≥„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ„Åù„ÅÆÂ§ú„ÄÅÁôªÂ±±ÂÆ∂„ÅØÁóÖÊ∞ó„Å´„Å™„Å£„Å¶„ÄÅÂàù„ÇÅ„Å¶ÊïëÊÄ•Ëªä„ÇíÈõªË©±„ÅßÂëº„Å≥„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇÁóÖÈô¢„Å´ÁùÄ„ÅÑ„Åü„Å®„Åç„ÄÅÂåªËÄÖ„ÅØË®Ä„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åó„Åü„ÄÇ„ÄåÈ£ü„Åπ„Çâ„Çå„Å™„ÅÑ„Ç≠„Éé„Ç≥„ÇíÈ£ü„Åπ„Åæ„Åó„Åü„Åã?„Ç≠„Éé„Ç≥„ÅØ„Å®„Å¶„ÇÇÂç±Èô∫„Å™„ÅÆ„Åß„ÄÅÊ∞ó„Çí‰ªò„Åë„Å¶„Åè„Å†„Åï„ÅÑ„ÄÇ„Åß„ÇÇ„ÄÅ„ÇÇ„ÅÜÂ§ß‰∏àÂ§´„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ„Åß„ÇÇ„ÄÅÁõÆ„ÅåÊÇ™„Åè„Å™„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇÁü•„Å£„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„Åó„Åü„Åã?‰ºë„Çì„Å†Êñπ„Åå„ÅÑ„ÅÑ„Åß„Åô„Çà„ÄÇ„Äç„Åù„Åó„Å¶„ÄÅÁôªÂ±±ÂÆ∂„ÅØÊØéÂπ¥ÁóÖÈô¢„Å´Ë°å„Å£„Å¶„ÄÅÂÅ•Â∫∑Ë®∫Êñ≠„ÇíÂèó„Åë„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ

A mountaineer lives in his hut in the mountains. He lives alone and has a very healthy life. Every morning, he goes on a hike for three hours. He grows vegetables and eats them. The mountaineer has never been to the hospital before. Because he lives a healthy life, he has never gotten sick. This afternoon, he goes to pick mushrooms in the mountains. The mountaineer knows a lot about mushrooms. There are mushrooms that are edible as well as mushrooms that are inedible. When he arrived at the hospital, the doctor said: ‚ÄúDid you eat inedible mushrooms? You have to be careful since mushrooms can be very dangerous. But everything is fine now. By the way, your eyes are getting weak. Did you know that? You should take a good rest.‚Äù Since then, the mountaineer goes to the hospital to receive a checkup every year
